<script>
/*AFF Chatter

 */
//===========================================================================
function AffChatter(username, token) {
  var _this = this;
  var HANDLE = username;
  var RECONNECT = 0;
  var STDRDELAY = Math.max(Math.floor(Math.random()*3000), 200);
  var RECONNECTDELAY = STDRDELAY;
  var NTRIES = 5;    //num tries
  var FTIMES = 1.7; //factor to increase the reconnect delay by
  var NODESRV = 'http://affchat1.adultfriendfinder.com/chat';
  var OK_TO_SEND = true;
  var mid = 0;
  var PINGER;
  var conv  = window.VIce && VIce.converse;
  var g = window.VIce && VIce.globals;
  var is_admin = g && g.admin == "1";
  var is_banned = false;
  var imc_error_alert = g && g.debug_cookie && g.debug_cookie.imc_error_alert;

 if (window.VIce && VIce.globals && VIce.globals.chat_con_url ){
     NODESRV = VIce.globals.chat_con_url;
 }
  // public functions
  _this.sendChatMessage = function(msgText, to, options) {
      options = options || {};
      mid++;
      var m_id = options.mid || mid;
      sockSend({ action: 'message', message: msgText, mid: m_id, to: to});
  };

  _this.sendActionMessage = function(action,to,options){
     options = options || {};
     var r_mid = options.rmid;
      if (action && to && r_mid) {
          sockSend({ action: action, to: to, rmid: r_mid});
      }
  };

 _this.sendIMNotification = function (n_txt, to , options){
     options = options || {};
     if (_.isString(n_txt) && _.isString(to)) {
         mid++;
         var m_id = options.mid || mid;
         sockSend({ action: 'chat_state', chat_state: n_txt, mid: mid, to: to});

         //sockSend({ action: 'chat_state', chat_state: n_txt, mid: mid, to: to, test: 1});
         //sockSend({ action: 'chat_state', message: n_txt, mid: mid, to: to});
     }

 };

 _this.reconnect = function(options){
     var port = 3022;
     options = options || {};
     if (options.reconnect) {
         RECONNECT = 1;
     }
     if (sock.readyState != 1) {
        console.log('Restarting...');
        sock = new SockJS(NODESRV);
        //sock = new SockJS('http://ki5111-30.friendfinderinc.com:3022/chat');
        sock.onopen = onOpen;
        sock.onclose = onClose;
        sock.onmessage = onMessage;
        sock.onerror = onError;
     }

 };


  // set up sock connection
  var sock = new SockJS(NODESRV);
  //var sock = new SockJS('http://ki5111-30.friendfinderinc.com:3022/chat');

  // sock connection private methods
  var onError = function(e) { if (is_admin && imc_error_alert) {alert("ERROR")} };
  var onOpen = function () {
    sockSend({ action: 'auth', room: HANDLE, reconnect: RECONNECT });
    if (RECONNECT) { RECONNECT = 0; }
  };

  var onClose = function(e) {
        clearInterval(PINGER);
        console.log("ERROR CODE: " + e);
        if (is_admin && imc_error_alert) {
            alert("Connection Closed" + e);
        }


      if (!is_banned) {
          RECONNECT = 1;
          if (RECONNECTDELAY < STDRDELAY * FTIMES * (NTRIES + 1)) {
              setTimeout(_this.reconnect, RECONNECTDELAY);
              RECONNECTDELAY = RECONNECTDELAY * FTIMES;
              console.log(RECONNECTDELAY);
          }

      }




   };

  var onMessage = function(e) {
    var rows = JSON.parse(e.data);
    var rlen = rows.length;
    var data,i;
      for(i = 0;i < rlen;i++) {
          data = rows[i];
          console.log("Message");
          console.log("============================");
          console.log(data);
          console.log("============================");
          switch(data.action) {
              case 'chat_info':
                  if (data.pingTimeoutMS) {
                      setPinger(data.pingTimeoutMS);
                  }
                  break;
              case 'message':
                  processReceipt(data);
                  if (conv && conv.receiveMessage) {
                      conv.receiveMessage(data);
                  }
                  break;
              case 'chat_state':
                  if (conv && conv.receiveMessage) {
                      conv.recieveIMNotification(data);
                  }
                  break;
              case 'bad_word':
                  if (data.to) {
                      data.handle = data.to;
                      conv.processReceipt(data);
                  }
                  break;
              case 'roster_add':
                  conv.updateRoster(data.users, {action: data.action});
                  break;
              case 'rr':
                  conv.processReceipt(data);
                  break;
              case 'roster_remove':
                  conv.updateRoster(data.users, {action: data.action});
                  break;
              case 'banned':
                  is_banned = true;
                  break;
              case 'user_connected':
                  RECONNECTDELAY = STDRDELAY;
                  break;
              case 'viewed':
                  conv.processViewed(data);
                  break;

              default:
                  break;
          };


      }
  };

  sock.onopen = onOpen;
  sock.onclose = onClose;
  sock.onmessage = onMessage;
  sock.onerror = onError;

  // Private methods
  var sockSend  = function(data) {
    if (OK_TO_SEND || data.action == 'user_ping') {
        console.log('sending', data);
        data.token = token;
        sock.send(JSON.stringify(data));
    }
  };

  var setPinger = function (interval) {
    sockSend({action: 'user_ping'});
    PINGER = setInterval(function() {
        sockSend({action: 'user_ping'});
    }, interval); // 5minutes
  };

  var sendGotMsg = function(to, rMid) { // Got Receipt
    sockSend({ action: 'gr', to: to, rmid: rMid});
  };

  var sendReadMsg = function(to, rMid) { // Read Receipt
    sockSend({ action: 'rr', to: to, rmid: rMid});
  };

  var processReceipt = function(msg) {
    if (msg.handle !== HANDLE) { // ignore messages from your self. though this shouldn't happen
        // for testing send both back now
        //sendGotMsg(msg.handle, msg.mid); // from and the mid
        sendReadMsg(msg.handle, msg.mid);
    }
  };

}
//===========================================================================




function initConverse() {

    var globals = VIce.globals || {},
        username = globals.own_handle,
        uid = globals.own_pwsid,
        session = globals.session,
        pass = "m_-^-_" + uid + "_-^-_who_-^-_" + session,
        sstorage_name = "converse_ignore_list",
        resource = "mobile#" + (new Date()).getTime() + '_' + Math.floor(Math.random() * 4294967295),
        menu_count = _.checkExists('VIce.globals.CountView.updateItemCount'),
        getNMsgCount,
        affChatter,
        conv;

    globals.main_domain = globals.main_domain || "adultfriendfinder.com";
    conv = this;
    conv.patterns = {
    system_messages: /^\[(exit_chat|enter_chat|exit_imc|waiting|invite|timeout|loggedout|decline|ignore|initiate_broadcast|invite_broadcast|webcam_off|webcam_on|webcam_accept|webcam_decline|welcome|stopping_broadcast|invitation_sent|invitation_cancelled|request_sent|request_failed|network_invite_accepted|network_invite_declined|now_friends|mobile_ignore|chatwindow)]$/,
    system_photo:  /^\[photo (http(s?):\/\/www\.(.+)\.com\/(.+)\/imc\/uploads\/(.+))]$/,
    system_webcam: /^\[webcam_invite (rtmp:\/\/(.+))]$/,
    system_invite: /^\[invite (.+)]$/
   };

    // new message count
    conv.nmsg_count = 0;


    function setVIceIMMenuCount(msg_count){
        msg_count = msg_count || 0;
        if ( !menu_count && _.checkExists('VIce.globals.CountView.updateItemCount') ) {
            menu_count = true;
        }
        if ( menu_count ) {
            VIce.globals.CountView.updateItemCount('member_chat', msg_count);
        }
    }



    conv.resetCount = function () {
        conv.nmsg_count = 0;
        setVIceIMMenuCount(conv.nmsg_count);
    };

    conv.incNMsgCount = function () {
        conv.nmsg_count = conv.nmsg_count || 0;
        conv.nmsg_count++;
        setVIceIMMenuCount(conv.nmsg_count);
    };
    conv.getNMsgCount2Digit = function () {
         var msg_count;
         msg_count =  conv.nmsg_count || " ";
         if( msg_count && isFinite(msg_count) && parseInt(msg_count,10) > 99){
             msg_count = "99+";
         }
        return msg_count;

    };

    conv.getNMsgCount = function(){
        var nmsg_count = 0,
            msg_chat_count = 0;
        if(conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.models && conv.chatboxes.length){
            _.each(conv.chatboxes.models, function ( tmp_md ) {
                if ( tmp_md ) {
                    msg_chat_count = tmp_md.get("unread_messages") || 0;
                    if( msg_chat_count && isFinite(msg_chat_count)){
                        nmsg_count = nmsg_count + parseInt(msg_chat_count,10);
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        conv.nmsg_count = nmsg_count;
        conv.emit("message_count", nmsg_count);
        setVIceIMMenuCount(conv.nmsg_count);
    };



    //get the chat handle
    conv.getChatHandle = function ( handle ) {
        var chat_handle = "",
            chat_host = "@chat-service." + globals.main_domain;
        if ( handle && _.isString(handle) ) {
            handle = handle.toLowerCase();
            if ( handle.indexOf(chat_host) > -1 ) {
                return handle;
            }
            chat_handle = handle + chat_host;
        }
        return chat_handle;
    };

    // get the conversation with the user with jid
    conv.getConversation = function ( handle ) {
        var conversation;
        handle = conv.getChatHandle(handle);
        if ( handle && _.isString(handle) ) {
            conversation = conv.chatboxes.get(handle);
        }
        return conversation;
    };

    //remove the chat from local storage
    conv.removeChatFromLocalStorage = function (temp_model){
        if ( temp_model
            && temp_model.messages
            && temp_model.messages.models
            && _.isArray(temp_model.messages.models)
            && temp_model.messages.localStorage
            && _.isFunction(temp_model.messages.localStorage.destroy)) {
            _.each(temp_model.messages.models, function ( tmp_md ) {
                if ( tmp_md ) {
                    temp_model.messages.localStorage.destroy(tmp_md);
                }
            });
            temp_model.messages.reset();
            if( conv.chatboxes && _.isFunction(conv.chatboxes.remove)){
                conv.chatboxes.remove(temp_model);
                if(conv.chatboxes.localStorage && _.isFunction(conv.chatboxes.localStorage.destroy)){
                  conv.chatboxes.localStorage.destroy(temp_model);
                }
            }
        }
    };
    //returns the model of the conversation deleted
    conv.deleteConversation = function ( handle ) {
        var temp_model = null;
        handle = handle || {};
        handle = conv.getChatHandle(handle);
        if ( handle && _.isString( handle ) ) {
            temp_model = conv.chatboxes.get(handle);
            if( temp_model ){
                conv.removeChatFromLocalStorage(temp_model);
                conv.emit("chats_removed");
            }
        }
        return temp_model;

    };

    //get the message from the conversation
    conv.getLastMessage = function ( handle ) {
        var last_message = "",
            conversation,
            l;
        handle = handle || {};
        conversation = conv.getConversation(handle);
        if ( conversation && conversation.messages && conversation.messages.length > 0 ) {
            l = conversation.messages.length;
            last_message = conversation.messages.models[l - 1].toJSON();
        }
        return last_message;
    };


    conv.addToIgnoreList = function ( handle ) {
        var on_ignore_list = false;
        handle = handle || {};
        handle = conv.getChatHandle(handle);
        if ( handle && _.isString(handle) ) {
            if ( conv.ignore_list && _.isArray(conv.ignore_list) ) {
                on_ignore_list = _.contains(conv.ignore_list, handle);
                if ( !on_ignore_list ) {
                    conv.ignore_list.push(handle);
                }
            } else {
                conv.ignore_list = [];
                conv.ignore_list.push(handle);
            }
        }
    };
    conv.updateIgnoreList = function () {
        var handle,
            ignore_list;
        if ( conv.banned_users_collection && conv.banned_users_collection.models ) {
            _.each(conv.banned_users_collection.models, function (model) {
                handle = model.get("banned_handle");
                if ( handle ) {
                    conv.addToIgnoreList(handle);
                }
            });
        }
        ignore_list = conv.getSessionIgnoreList();
        if( ignore_list && _.isArray(ignore_list) && ignore_list ){
            conv.ignore_list = conv.ignore_list || [];
            if( _.isArray(conv.ignore_list)){
                conv.ignore_list = _.union(conv.ignore_list, ignore_list);
            }
        }

    };
    conv.saveIgnoreList = function(){
        if ( _.returnValue('VIce.$.support.session_storage', 0) && conv.ignore_list ){
             window.sessionStorage.setItem(sstorage_name,JSON.stringify(conv.ignore_list));
        }
    };


    conv.getSessionIgnoreList = function () {
        var ignore_list = null;
        if ( _.returnValue('VIce.$.support.session_storage', 0) ) {
            ignore_list = window.sessionStorage.getItem(sstorage_name);
            if ( ignore_list && _.isString(ignore_list) ) {
                try {
                    ignore_list = JSON.parse(ignore_list);
                } catch ( e ) {
                    ignore_list = null;
                }
            }
        }
        return ignore_list;
    };

    conv.getBannedUsers = function () {
        if ( !conv.banned_users_colelction && (window.VIce && VIce.collection && _.isFunction(VIce.collection)) ) {
            conv.banned_users_collection = VIce.collection("IMCBannedUsers");
        }
        if ( conv.banned_users_collection && _.isFunction(conv.banned_users_collection.getUsers) ) {
            conv.banned_users_collection.on("add_complete", conv.updateIgnoreList);
            conv.banned_users_collection.reset();
            conv.banned_users_collection.getUsers();
        }

    };

    conv.onConnect = function (status, condition, reconnect) {
            if( status ){
                conv.current_status = status;
                conv.emit("status_update", status);
            }
            if ((status === Strophe.Status.CONNECTED) ||
                (status === Strophe.Status.ATTACHED)) {
                if ((typeof reconnect !== 'undefined') && (reconnect)) {
                    conv.log(status === Strophe.Status.CONNECTED ? 'Reconnected' : 'Reattached');
                    conv.onReconnected();
                } else {
                    conv.log(status === Strophe.Status.CONNECTED ? 'Connected' : 'Attached');
                    conv.onConnected();
                }
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.DISCONNECTED) {
                // TODO: Handle case where user manually logs out...
                conv.log("VICE IM DISCONNECTED");
                if (conv.auto_reconnect) {
                    conv.reconnect();
                }
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.Error) {
               conv.log("VICE IM CONNECTION ERROR");
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.CONNECTING) {
                conv.log("VICE IM CONNECTING");
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.CONNFAIL) {
                conv.log("VICE IM CONNECTION FAIL");
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.AUTHENTICATING) {
                conv.log("VICE IM Authenticating");
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.AUTHFAIL) {
                conv.log("VICE IM Authentication Failed");
            } else if (status === Strophe.Status.DISCONNECTING) {
                conv.log("VICE IM DISCONNECTING");
            }
        };

    //send presence message
    conv.sendPresence = function ( priority_t ) {
        priority_t =  "10"; // this way not a fight with desktop
        if ( !isFinite(priority_t) ) {
            priority_t = "10";
        }
        if ( conv.connection && _.isFunction(conv.connection.send) && window.$pres && _.isFunction(window.$pres) ) {
            conv.connection.send(window.$pres().c("priority").t(priority_t));
        }
    };


    conv.createMessage = function(m_from, m_to, m_text, mid) {
        var timestamp = (new Date()).getTime(),
            sys_message = null;

        mid = mid || timestamp;
        //m_text = m_text || ("" + timestamp);
        if (_.checkExists("VIce.converse.getChatHandle") && _.isFunction(VIce.converse.getChatHandle)) {
            m_from = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(m_from);
            m_to = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(m_to);
        }
        if (m_text && _.isString(m_text) && m_from && m_to) {
            if (window.$msg && _.isFunction(window.$msg)) {
                sys_message = window.$msg({from: m_from, to: m_to, type: 'chat', id: mid})
                    .c('body').t(m_text).up()
                    .c('active', {'xmlns': 'http://jabber.org/protocol/chatstates'});
            }
        }
        return sys_message;
    };






    //extend converse views and collections
    if ( conv.ControlBoxView && conv.ChatBoxView && conv.ChatBox && conv.ChatBoxes ) {
        //get the banned users;
        conv.getBannedUsers();
        //empty controlbox
        var FFControlBoxView = conv.ControlBoxView.extend({
            render: function () {
                //overwrite the render function with empty function
            }
        });


        //overwrite the message view
        var FFView = conv.ChatBoxView.extend({
            showMessage: function ( t ) {
                //overwrite the showMessage function with empty function
            },
            onMessageAdded: function ( message ) {
                var unread_messages,
                    last_message_time = "",
                    chat_status;

                //update the chat statuses
                chat_status = this.model.get('chat_status') || "";
                //increment the number of new messages
                if ( (message.get('sender') != 'me') ) {

                    if ( chat_status === "sent" ) {
                        this.model.set("chat_active", true);
                    }
                    unread_messages = this.model.get("unread_messages") || 0;
                    unread_messages = unread_messages + 1;
                    this.model.set("unread_messages", unread_messages);
                    this.model.set("chat_status", "incoming");

                } else {
                    if ( chat_status === "incoming" ) {
                        this.model.set("chat_active", true);
                        this.model.set("chat_request", false);
                    }
                    this.model.set("chat_status", "sent");
                }

                if ( this.model ) {
                    last_message_time = this.model.get("last_message_time");
                }
                if ( last_message_time && _.isFunction(message.get) ) {
                    if ( last_message_time === message.get("time") ) {
                        //messages already viewed reset the count
                        this.model.set("unread_messages", 0);
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        var FFChatBox = conv.ChatBox.extend({
            initialize: function () {
                this.on("send_message", this.sendIMMessage);
                this.on("send_viewed", this.sendViewed);
                this.on("send_notification", this.sendIMNotification);
                this.on("focus",this.focusChatBox);
                conv.ChatBox.prototype.initialize.apply(this, arguments);
            },
            focusChatBox: function(){
                var i, l,
                    m_id,
                    not_viewed_msgs;
                if (this.messages && this.messages.where ){
                    not_viewed_msgs = this.messages.where({not_viewed: 1});
                    if(not_viewed_msgs && not_viewed_msgs.length){
                        for(i=0;i<not_viewed_msgs.length;i++){
                           not_viewed_msgs[i].set("not_viewed", 0);
                           m_id = not_viewed_msgs[i].get('m_id');
                           this.sendViewed(m_id);
                        }

                    }

                }


                this.set('focused',1);


            },
            sendIMMessage: function ( text, options ) {
                var m_id,
                    handle,
                    chat_msg;


                options = options || {};


                if ( !options.my_jid ) {
                    //get  my_jid
                     options.my_jid = conv.connection.jid;
                }
                if ( !options.bare_jid ) {
                    options.bare_jid = this.get("jid");
                }

                if (conv && conv.sendChatMessage){
                    handle = conv.getHandle(options.bare_jid);
                    conv.sendChatMessage(handle,text,{mid: options.m_id});
                }

                if (text && _.isString(text) && options.my_jid && options.bare_jid) {
                    m_id = options.m_id || (new Date()).getTime();
                    if (window.$msg && _.isFunction(window.$msg)) {
                        chat_msg = window.$msg({from: options.my_jid, to: options.bare_jid, type: 'chat', id: m_id})
                            .c('body').t(text).up()
                            .c('active', {'xmlns': 'http://jabber.org/protocol/chatstates'});
                    }
                    /*if (conv.connection && conv.connection.send && _.isFunction(conv.connection.send)) {
                        if (!options.sys_msg && conv.connection.receipts && _.isFunction(conv.connection.receipts.sendMessage)) {
                            conv.connection.receipts.sendMessage(chat_msg);
                        } else {
                            conv.connection.send(chat_msg);
                        }

                    }*/

                }
            },
            sendViewed: function(mid, options){

                options = options || {};
                var handle;

                if ( !options.my_jid ) {
                    //get  my_jid
                     options.my_jid = conv.connection.jid;
                }
                if ( !options.bare_jid ) {
                    options.bare_jid = this.get("jid");
                }

                if (conv && conv.sendViewedMessage && mid){
                    handle = conv.getHandle(options.bare_jid);
                    conv.sendViewedMessage(handle,{rmid:mid});
                }


            },
            sendIMNotification: function ( text ) {
                var notify,
                    handle,
                    bare_jid;
                if ( text && _.isString(text) ) {
                    bare_jid = this.get('jid');
                    if (conv && conv.sendChatMessage) {
                        handle = conv.getHandle(bare_jid);
                        conv.sendIMNotification(handle, text);
                    }
                   /* if ( bare_jid && _.isString(bare_jid) ) {
                        if (window.$msg && _.isFunction(window.$msg)) {
                            notify = $msg({'to': bare_jid, 'type': 'chat'})
                                .c(text, {'xmlns': 'http://jabber.org/protocol/chatstates'});
                        }
                        if ( notify && conv.connection && _.isFunction(conv.connection.send) ) {
                            conv.connection.send(notify);
                            return true;
                        }

                    }*/
                }
            }
        });

        var FFChatBoxes = conv.ChatBoxes.extend({
            model: FFChatBox,
            initialize: function () {
                this.on("node_message", this.onMessage);
                this.on("node_notification", this.onNotification);

                conv.ChatBoxes.prototype.initialize.apply(this, arguments);
            },

            registerMessageHandler: function () {
                /*conv.connection.addHandler(
                    jQuery.proxy(function ( message ) {
                        this.onMessage(message);
                        return true;
                    }, this), null, 'message', 'chat');*/
            },
            onNotification: function(data) {
                var chatbox,
                    jid;

                data = data || {};

                if (data.handle && data.chat_state) {
                    jid = conv.getChatHandle(data.handle);
                    if (jid) {
                        chatbox = this.get(jid);
                        if (chatbox) {
                            switch(data.chat_state) {
                                case 'composing':
                                    chatbox.trigger('composing', data);
                                    break
                                default:
                                    chatbox.trigger('action', data);
                                    break;

                            }
                        }
                    }

                }

            },
            onMessage: function ( message ) {
                var buddy_jid,
                    mtch,
                    focused,
                    on_ignore_list = false,
                    el_message = $(message),
                    message_from = el_message.attr('from'),
                    m_id = el_message.attr('id'),
                    body = el_message.children('body').text(),
                    composing = el_message.find('composing'),
                    el_forwarded = el_message.children('forwarded'),
                    el_received = el_message.children('received'),
                    el_viewed = el_message.children('viewed'),
                    received_msg = null,
                    received_id,
                    from,
                    to,
                    chatbox;

                if ( message_from === conv.connection.jid ) {
                    // FIXME: Forwarded messages should be sent to specific resources,
                    // not broadcasted
                    return true;
                }
                if ( el_forwarded.length ) {
                    el_message = el_forwarded.children('message');
                } else if ( el_received.length && el_received.attr('xmlns') === 'urn:xmpp:carbons:2' ) {
                    el_message = el_message.children('received').children('forwarded').children('message');
                    message_from = el_message.attr('from');
                }

                from = Strophe.getBareJidFromJid(message_from);
                to = Strophe.getBareJidFromJid(el_message.attr('to'));

                if ( from == conv.bare_jid ) {
                    // I am the sender, so this must be a forwarded message...
                    buddy_jid = to;
                } else {
                    buddy_jid = from;
                }
                buddy_jid = buddy_jid.toLowerCase();
                chatbox = this.get(buddy_jid);

                // check if the user is blocked or in the ingnore list
                if ( conv.ignore_list && _.isArray(conv.ignore_list) && conv.ignore_list.length > 0 ) {
                    on_ignore_list = _.contains(conv.ignore_list, buddy_jid.toLowerCase());
                    if ( on_ignore_list ) {
                        console.log("User is blocked: " + buddy_jid);
                        return;
                    }
                }

                if (chatbox) {
                    if (chatbox.messages && chatbox.messages.length > 0){
                        if (el_received && el_received.length) {
                            received_id = el_received.attr('id');
                            if (received_id) {
                                received_msg = chatbox.messages.findWhere({m_id: received_id});
                                if (received_msg && received_msg.set) {
                                    received_msg.set("delivered", 1);
                                    try {
                                        chatbox.messages.localStorage.update(received_msg);

                                    } catch(e) {

                                    }
                                    chatbox.trigger("message_delivered", received_id);

                                }
                            }

                        }else if (el_viewed && el_viewed.length) {
                            received_id = el_viewed.attr('id');
                            if (received_id) {
                                received_msg = chatbox.messages.findWhere({m_id: received_id});
                                if (received_msg && received_msg.set) {
                                    received_msg.set("viewed", 1);
                                    try {
                                        chatbox.messages.localStorage.update(received_msg);

                                    } catch(e) {

                                    }
                                    chatbox.trigger("message_viewed", received_id);
                                }
                            }

                        }

                    }


                    chatbox.trigger("message_received", message);
                    if (!body) {
                        if (composing.length) {
                            chatbox.trigger('composing', message);
                        } else {
                            chatbox.trigger("action", message);
                        }
                        return;
                    }
                } else if (!body){
                    return;
                }

                if (conv.patterns) {
                     mtch = conv.patterns.system_messages.exec(body);
                    if ( mtch ) {
                        //if not an invite
                        if(mtch.indexOf("invite") < 0){
                          return;
                        }
                    } else {
                        mtch = conv.patterns.system_webcam.exec(body);
                        if (!mtch) {
                            mtch = conv.patterns.system_invite.exec(body);
                        }
                    }
                }



                // if the chat does not exist with the user creat it
                if ( !chatbox ) {
                    chatbox = this.create({
                        'id': buddy_jid,
                        'jid': buddy_jid,
                        'fullname': buddy_jid,
                        'image_type': "",
                        'image': "",
                        'focused': "",
                        'url': "",
                        'chat_request': true,
                        'chat_time': (new Date()).getTime()
                    });
                }

                // if any sort of invite we don't accept sent mobile_ignore
                if (mtch) {
                   chatbox.trigger("send_message", '[mobile_ignore]',{sys_msg: 1});
                   //chatbox.trigger("send_message", '[webcam_decline]');
                } else {
                    chatbox.receiveMessage(el_message);
                    focused = chatbox.get("focused");
                    received_msg = chatbox.messages.models[chatbox.messages.length-1];
                     if (received_msg && received_msg.set) {
                         received_msg.set("m_id", m_id);
                         received_msg.set("not_viewed", 1);
                         if (focused ) {
                            received_msg.set("not_viewed", 0);
                            chatbox.trigger("send_viewed",m_id);
                         }
                     }


                    //message received send waiting message
                   // chatbox.trigger("send_message", '[waiting]',{sys_msg: 1});
                }


                // trigger onMessage
                conv.emit('onMessage', message);
                return true;
            },
            onConnected:  function () {
                this.localStorage = new Backbone.LocalStorage(
                    hex_sha1('converse.chatboxes-'+ conv.bare_jid));
                if (!this.get('controlbox')) {
                    this.add({
                        id: 'controlbox',
                        box_id: 'controlbox'
                    });
                } else {
                    this.get('controlbox').save();
                }
                // This line below will make sure the Roster is set up
                //this.get('controlbox').set({connected:true});
                this.registerMessageHandler();
                // Get cached chatboxes from localstorage
                this.fetch({
                    add: true,
                    success: $.proxy(function (collection, resp) {
                        if (_.include(_.pluck(resp, 'id'), 'controlbox')) {
                            // If the controlbox was saved in localstorage, it must be visible
                            this.get('controlbox').set({visible:true}).save();
                        }
                    }, this)
                });
            }
        });


        // get the new message count
        getNMsgCount =  _.debounce(conv.getNMsgCount, 300);
        conv.on("onMessage",  getNMsgCount );
        conv.on("chats_removed", getNMsgCount );

        conv.chatboxes = new FFChatBoxes();
        conv.ControlBoxView = FFControlBoxView;
        conv.ChatBoxView = FFView;
        conv.chatboxesview = new conv.ChatBoxesView({model: conv.chatboxes});


        //connect to IMC
       // username = username + '@chat-service.' + globals.main_domain + '/' + resource;
        //conv.connection = new Strophe.Connection(conv.bosh_service_url);
          conv.connection = {};



        // no connection
       // conv.connection.connect(username, pass, conv.onConnect);


        //connected
        if(!conv.bare_jid){
            conv.bare_jid = conv.getChatHandle(username);
        }

        if(!conv.roster){
            conv.roster = new Backbone.Collection();
        }
        if(conv.connection && !conv.connection.connected){
            conv.connection.connected = true;
        }

        if (conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.onConnected){
            conv.chatboxes.onConnected();
        }


        //affChat
        //-------------------------------------------------
        function connectToChat(data) {
            if (data && username) {
                username = username.toLowerCase();
                affChatter = new AffChatter(username, data);
            }

            if (conv.cleanup_interval) {
                clearInterval(conv.cleanup_interval);
            }
            conv.cleanup_interval = window.setInterval(cleanupIncomingChats, 60 * 1000);

        }

        conv.connectToNode = function() {
            VIce.$.ajax({
                url: "/coreapi/imc?_=" + new Date().getTime(),
                method: "POST",
                data: { action: 'get_web_token'}
            }).done(connectToChat)
                .fail(function() {
                    console.log("Failed")
                });

        };



        conv.processReceipt = function(data){
            data = data || {};
            var handle = data.handle,
                mid = data.rmid,
                timestamp = (new Date()).getTime()+"",
                req,
                m_to,
                m_from,
                m_receipt;
            if (mid && handle && window.$msg){
                m_to = VIce.converse.bare_jid;
                m_from = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(handle);
                m_receipt = window.$msg({to: m_to, from: m_from, id: timestamp});
                req  = window.Strophe.xmlElement('received', {'xmlns': "urn:xmpp:receipts", 'id': mid});
                m_receipt.tree().appendChild(req);
                console.log(m_receipt);
                if (conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.trigger && m_receipt && m_receipt.nodeTree) {
                    //conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_notification", data);
                    conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_message", m_receipt.nodeTree);
                }
            }

        };

        conv.processViewed = function(data){
            data = data || {};
            var handle = data.handle,
                mid = data.rmid,
                timestamp = (new Date()).getTime()+"",
                req,
                m_to,
                m_from,
                m_viewed;
            if (mid && handle && window.$msg){
                m_to = VIce.converse.bare_jid;
                m_from = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(handle);
                m_viewed = window.$msg({to: m_to, from: m_from, id: timestamp});
                req  = window.Strophe.xmlElement('viewed', {'xmlns': "urn:xmpp:receipts", 'id': mid});
                m_viewed.tree().appendChild(req);
                if (conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.trigger && m_viewed && m_viewed.nodeTree) {
                    //conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_notification", data);
                    conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_message", m_viewed.nodeTree);
                }
            }

        };



        conv.sendViewedMessage = function(to, options) {
            if (affChatter && affChatter.sendActionMessage) {
                affChatter.sendActionMessage('viewed',to,options);
            }
        };

        conv.sendChatMessage = function(to, msg_text, options) {
            if (affChatter && affChatter.sendChatMessage) {
                affChatter.sendChatMessage(msg_text, to, options);
            }
        };

        conv.sendIMNotification= function(to, n_msg){
            if (affChatter && affChatter.sendChatMessage) {
                affChatter.sendIMNotification(n_msg, to);
            }
        };

        conv.createMessage = function(m_from, m_to, m_text, mid){
            var timestamp = (new Date()).getTime(),
                chat_message = null;
            //m_text = m_text || ("" + timestamp);
            mid = mid || timestamp;
            if (_.checkExists("VIce.converse.getChatHandle") && _.isFunction(VIce.converse.getChatHandle)) {
                m_from = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(m_from);
                m_to = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(m_to);
            }
            if (m_text && _.isString(m_text) && m_from && m_to) {
                if (window.$msg && _.isFunction(window.$msg)) {
                    chat_message = window.$msg({from: m_from, to: m_to, type: 'chat', id: mid})
                        .c('body').t(m_text).up()
                        .c('active', {'xmlns': 'http://jabber.org/protocol/chatstates'});
                }
            }
            return chat_message;
        };


        conv.receiveMessage = function(data){
            var chat_message;
            chat_message = conv.createMessage(data.handle,conv.bare_jid, data.message, data.mid);
            if (chat_message && chat_message.nodeTree && conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.trigger) {
                conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_message", chat_message.nodeTree);
            }
        };

        conv.recieveIMNotification = function(data){
            var notify_msg,
                handle;

                data = data || {};

            if (data.handle && data.chat_state ) {
                handle = VIce.converse.getChatHandle(data.handle);
                notify_msg = $msg({'from': handle, 'type': 'chat'})
                    .c(data.chat_state, {'xmlns': 'http://jabber.org/protocol/chatstates'});
                if (conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.trigger && notify_msg && notify_msg.nodeTree) {
                    //conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_notification", data);
                    conv.chatboxes.trigger("node_message", notify_msg.nodeTree);
                }

            }


        };



        conv.getHandle = function(chat_handle){
            var handle = chat_handle,
                ind,
                chat_host = "@chat-service." + globals.main_domain;
            if ( handle ){
                ind = handle.indexOf(chat_host);
                if(ind > 1){
                    handle = handle.substring(0,ind);
                }

            }

            return handle;
        };

        conv.updateRoster = function(users,options){
            var i,
                l,
                ext_model,
                tmp_model;
            options = options || {};
            if (users && _.isArray(users) && users.length && conv.roster){
                l = users.length;
                for(i = 0; i < l; i++) {
                    ext_model = conv.roster.where({user_id: users[i]});
                    if (options.action == 'roster_remove') {
                        if (ext_model && ext_model.length) {
                            conv.roster.remove(ext_model);
                        }
                    } else if (!(ext_model && ext_model.length)) {
                        conv.roster.add({user_id: users[i], "chat_status": "online"});
                    }

                }
               conv.emit('onRoster');
            }

        };


        window.VIce = VIce || {};
        VIce.converse = conv;

        conv.connectToNode();
    }


}
function cleanupIncomingChats() {
    var curr_time = (new Date()).getTime(),
        time_interval = 120 * 1000,
        chats_removed = false,
        conv,
        chat_time;

    function destroyInactive ( temp_model ) {
        if ( temp_model && _.isFunction(temp_model.get) && temp_model.get("chat_request") && !temp_model.get("chat_active") ) {
            chat_time = temp_model.get('chat_time');
            if ( chat_time && isFinite(chat_time) ) {
                if ( curr_time - parseInt(chat_time, 10) > time_interval ) {
                    chats_removed = true;
                    if ( temp_model.messages && temp_model.messages.models && temp_model.messages.localStorage ) {
                        _.each(temp_model.messages.models, function ( tmp_message ) {
                            if ( tmp_message ) {
                                temp_model.messages.localStorage.destroy(tmp_message);
                            }
                        });
                        temp_model.messages.reset();
                        conv.chatboxes.remove(temp_model);
                        if ( conv.chatboxes.localStorage && _.isFunction(conv.chatboxes.localStorage.destroy) ) {
                            conv.chatboxes.localStorage.destroy(temp_model);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if ( _.checkExists("VIce.converse") ) {
        conv = VIce.converse;
        conv.time_cleaned = (new Date()).getTime();
        //conv.sendPresence();
        if ( conv.chatboxes && conv.chatboxes.models && conv.chatboxes.length ) {
            _.each(conv.chatboxes.models, destroyInactive);
            //if any chats removed trigger chats_removed
            if ( chats_removed ) {
                conv.emit("chats_removed");
            }
        }
    }
}
</script>

             (function() {
        VIce.setRole('right-menu', VIce.extend('role', 'menu', {
            events : {
                'click a' : 'linkIsClicked'
            },
            checkPageMenuMode : function  () {
                var page = VIce.currentPage();

                if (page.menu_mode && page.menu_mode === 'on') {
                    this.hide();
                    page.menu_mode = 'off';
                } else if (!page.menu_mode || page.menu_mode === 'off') {
                    this.show();
                    page.menu_mode = 'on';

                }
            },
            viceInit: function () {
                var $window = VIce.$(window),
                    width = $window.width(),
                    move_width,
                    menu = this,
                    found_main_view = false,
                    complied_tmpl;

                function checkModeProxy() {
                    menu.checkPageMenuMode();
                }

                this.vars = {};
                this.views = [];
                this.menu_overlay = this.$el.find('[data-context="menu-overlay"]');
                this.menu_content = this.$el.find('[data-context="menu-content"]');
                this.menu_wrapper = this.$el.find('> .relative');
                this.hide_duration = 350;
                this.show_duration = 300;
                this.transition_type = "ease-out";
                this.is_wp = VIce.$.os && VIce.$.os.wp;

                this.menu_overlay.on('click', checkModeProxy);
                this.hidden = true;

                function getPageView(ele) {
                    var view = ele.attr("data-view");
                    return VIce.view(view, {el: ele});
                }

                function bindInlineHandler(view) {
                    var _e = view.e_to_bind, _page;
                    if (_e) {
                        if (_e.tmpl) {
                            view.tmpl = _e.tmpl;
                        }
                        if (view.ele_options && view.ele_options.default_value) {
                            var d = {};
                            d[_e.prop] = view.ele_options.default_value;
                            view[_e.action](d);
                        }
                        _page = menu.vars[_e.target];
                        if (_page && _page.prop_model) {
                            _page.prop_model.on(_e.event || 'change' + ':' + _e.prop,
                                function () {
                                    var d = {};
                                    d[_e.prop] = _page.prop_model.get(_e.prop);
                                    view[_e.action](d);
                                },
                                _page);
                        }
                    }
                }

                function attachViewEvents(new_vars, trigger_right_away) {
                    var page = menu;
                    if (!new_vars) {
                        new_vars = page.vars;
                    }

                    function attachViewEvent(view) {
                        var args = view.e_to_bind, page_el, d;
                        //console.warn("attachViewEvents", args);
                        if (args) {
                            if (!args.prop) {
                                VIce.trigger("missing", {
                                    'type': 'argument',
                                    'name': 'args.prop',
                                    'function': 'Page.attachViewEvent'
                                });
                            }

                            if (args.tmpl) {
                                view.tmpl = args.tmpl;
                            }

                            if (args.target == 'Page') {
                                page_el = page;
                            } else if (args.target == 'View') {
                                page_el = view;
                            } else if (args.target == 'Parent') {
                                page_el = view.parent_view || view.options.parent_view;
                            } else if (args.target) {
                                page_el = page.vars[args.target];
                            }
                            if (page_el && page_el.prop_model) {
                                if (view.ele_options
                                    && view.ele_options.default_value
                                    && _.isUndefined(page_el.prop_model.get(args.prop))
                                ) {
                                    d = {};
                                    d[args.prop] = view.ele_options.default_value;
                                    page_el.prop_model.set(d);
                                }
                                if (trigger_right_away
                                    || !_.isUndefined(page_el.prop_model.get(args.prop))
                                ) {
                                    view[args.action](page_el.prop_model.toJSON(), args);
                                }
                                page_el.prop_model.on('change' + ':' + args.prop,
                                    function () {
                                        //var d = {};
                                        //d[_e.prop] = page_el.prop_model.get(_e.prop);
                                        view[args.action](page_el.prop_model.toJSON(), args);
                                    }, page_el);
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    _.each(new_vars, attachViewEvent);
                }

                function setMenuRoles(i, ele) {
                    ele = VIce.$(ele);
                    var role = ele.attr("data-role"),
                        data_name = ele.attr('data-name'),
                        object = {},
                        load_src,
                        page = menu,
                        compiled_tmpl;

                    function setHandler(event_string, i) {
                        var event = VIce.getViewEvents(event_string);
                        //console.warn(event);

                        if (event.prop === "event") {
                            page.on(event.target, VIce.$.proxy(object[event.action], object));
                        } else if (event) {
                            event.tmpl = compiled_tmpl;
                            console.warn(event, event.tmpl);
                            page.vars[data_name].e_to_bind = event;
                            attachViewEvents([
                                page.vars[data_name]
                            ]);
                        }
                    }

                    if (role !== 'view') {
                        if (role === "load_src") {
                            load_src = ele.attr("data-load-src");
                            if (load_src && _.isString(load_src)) {
                                load_src = decodeURIComponent(load_src);
                                ele.attr('src', load_src);
                            }
                            return;
                        }
                        if (!data_name) {
                            data_name = role + i;
                        }
                        object = VIce.role(role, {'el': ele, parent_role_obj: menu});

                        if (!object) {
                            object = ele;
                        }

                        if (!(role == 'body' || role == 'header' || role == 'footer')) {
                            menu.vars[data_name] = object;
                        }

                    } else {
                        object = getPageView(ele);
                        if (object) {

                            if (!data_name) {
                                data_name = ele.attr('data-view') + i;
                            }
                            if (object._main_view) {
                                found_main_view = true;
                            }
                            menu.on("beforepageshow", function () {
                                object._beforePageShow();
                            });
                            menu.on("afterpagehide", function () {
                                object._afterPageHide();
                            });
                            menu.views.push(object);
                        }
                    }
                    if (object) {
                        object.name = data_name;
                        menu.vars[data_name] = object;
                    }

                    if (ele.attr('data-events')) {
                        complied_tmpl = _.template(ele.html());
                        _.each(ele.attr('data-events').split(','), setHandler);
                    }
                }

                function updateMenuWidth(d) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        width = (d && d.width) || $window.width();
                        move_width = Math.min(parseInt((width * 0.75), 10), 350);
                        menu.menu_content.css({'width': move_width + 'px', 'float': 'right'});
                        menu.menu_overlay.css({'width': (width - move_width) + 'px', 'float': 'left'});
                        menu.$el.css({'width': width + 'px'});
                        if (menu.hidden) {
                            menu.$el.animate({'translate3d': (width) + 'px,0,0'}, 0);
                        }
                    }, 100);
                }

                updateMenuWidth();
                menu.$el.css({'translate3d': (width) + 'px,0,0', 'display': 'block'});

                VIce.once('pagechanged', function () {

                    menu.height = menu.$el.height();
                    // menu.$el.css({'height': menu.height + 'px'});
                    // menu.menu_wrapper.css({'height': menu.height + 'px'});
                    menu.menu_overlay.css({'height': menu.height + 'px'});

                    if (!menu.roles_set) {
                        menu.$el.find("[data-role]").each(setMenuRoles);
                        _.each(menu.vars, bindInlineHandler);

                        menu.vars.VIce = VIce;
                        menu.vars.Page = menu;
                        menu.roles_set = 1;
                    }

                    if (!found_main_view) {
                        if (menu.views[0]) {
                            menu.views[0]._main_view = true;
                        }
                    }

                    VIce.parseViewIcons(menu.$el);
                    VIce.on('vice_orientationchange', updateMenuWidth);
                });

                menu.on('_first_load_trigger', function () {
                    menu.first_load = 1;
                    menu.off('_first_load_trigger');
                    menu.trigger('beforepageshow');
                });
            },
            reset : function () {
                var conf = {},
                    _s = VIce.screen,
                    min_height = (_s && _s.height && _s.width) ? ( (_s.height > _s.width) ? _s.width : _s.height) : VIce.$(window).height(),
                    page = VIce.currentPage();

                if (VIce.$.support.overflow_hidden) {
                    conf.overflow = '';
                    conf.height = 'auto';
                }

                conf['min-height'] = min_height + 'px';
                page.css(conf);
                // need to make sure sidenav edges wont be visible on the page when changing device orientation
                //this.$el.css({'visibility' : 'hidden'});
                this.$el.animate({ 'translate3d': (VIce.screen.width) + 'px,0,0' }, 0);
                this.hidden = true;
                page.menu_mode = "off";
            },
            show: function () {
                var $window = VIce.$(window),
                    width = $window.width(),
                    move_width = Math.min(parseInt((width * 0.75), 10), 350),
                    menu = this;
                function resizePage() {
                    if (VIce.$.support.overflow_hidden) {
                        VIce.currentPage().css({'height': menu.$el.height() + 'px', 'overflow': 'hidden'});
                    }
                    VIce.trigger("menu_open");
                }

                menu.$el.animate({'translate3d': '0px,0,0'}, menu.show_duration, menu.transition_type, resizePage);

                if (menu.is_wp) {
                    setTimeout(resizePage, 2 * menu.show_duration);
                }

                menu.hidden = false;
                if (!menu.first_load) {
                    menu.trigger('_first_load_trigger');
                }
            },
            hide: function () {
                var menu = this;

                function _resetMenu () {
                    menu.reset();
                }
                menu.$el.animate({ 'translate3d': (VIce.screen.width) + 'px,0,0' }, menu.hide_duration, menu.transition_type, _resetMenu);

                if (menu.is_wp) {
                    setTimeout(_resetMenu, 2*menu.hide_duration);
                }
            }
        }));
        var TempVanilla = (function () {
            var menus = {};
            function toggleMenu(menu_id) {
                if (menus[menu_id]) {
                    if (menus[menu_id].hidden) {
                        menus[menu_id].show();
                    } else {
                        menus[menu_id].hide();
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn('VIce.toggleMenu->' + menu_id + "doesn't exist");
                }
            }
            function getMenu(menu_id) {
                if (menus[menu_id]) {
                    return menus[menu_id];
                } else {
                    console.warn('VIce.getMenu-> ' + menu_id + " doesn't exist");
                }
            }
            function hideMenu(menu_id) {
                if (menus[menu_id]) {
                    menus[menu_id].hide();
                } else {
                    console.warn('VIce.hideMenu->' + menu_id + " doesn't exist");
                }
            }

            function showMenu(menu_id) {
                if (menus[menu_id]) {
                    menus[menu_id].show();
                } else {
                    console.warn('VIce.showMenu->' + menu_id + " doesn't exist");
                }
            }

            function activateMenu () {
                //VIce.currentPage().trigger('check_menu_mode');
                menus.menu && menus.menu.checkPageMenuMode();
            }

            function resetMenus () {
                var n;
                for (n in menus) {
                    if (menus.hasOwnProperty(n)) {
                        if (menus[n].reset && _.isFunction(menus[n].reset)) {
                            menus[n].reset();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            VIce.$("div[data-role=right-menu]").each(function (i, ele) {
                var menu_ele = VIce.$(ele);
                var menu_id = menu_ele.attr('id');
                menus[menu_id] = VIce.role('right-menu',{'el': menu_ele});
            });
            return _.extend({
                // 'name': 'TempVanilla',
                'showMenu': showMenu,
                'hideMenu': hideMenu,
                'toggleMenu': toggleMenu,
                'getMenu': getMenu,
                'activateMenu' : activateMenu,
                'resetMenus' : resetMenus
            }, Backbone.Events);
        })();
        VIce.$.extend(VIce, TempVanilla);
    })();
    
});
(function () {
    var langChangeFunc = function () {
        var page = VIce.currentPage();
        var sel;
        if(page && page.find){
          sel = page.find('#language-change');
        }
        if(sel && sel.length){
          sel = sel[0];
        } else{
          sel = document.getElementById("language-change");
        }
        function makeAjaxCall(method, url, async) {
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open(method, url, async);
            xhr.send();
        }

        function handleLanguageChange() {
            var selectedStr = sel.options[sel.selectedIndex].value,
                lang = selectedStr.split("=").pop(),
                url = '/coreapi/session?action=set_lang&lang=' + lang;
            makeAjaxCall("GET", url, true);
            window.location.replace(selectedStr);
        }
        if(sel) {
            sel.addEventListener("change", handleLanguageChange, false);
        }
    };
    if (window.VIce && VIce.on) {
        VIce.on('pagechanged', langChangeFunc);
    }
})();

             (function () {
                if (window.VIce && VIce.on) {
                    VIce.on("pagechanged", function () {
                        var hash = window.location.hash;
                        if (hash.indexOf('#main')== 0){
                            window.location.replace('/www/spa/');
                        }else if(hash.indexOf('#search') == 0){
                             window.location.replace('/www/spa/');
                        }else if(hash.indexOf('#search_results') == 0){
                             window.location.replace('/www/spa/');
                        }else if(hash.indexOf('#live_action') == 0){
                             window.location.replace('/www/spa/#/live_action/online');
                        }
                    });
                }
            })();

    function getAgeOptions (start, end) {
        start = start || 18;
        end = end || 99;
        var i, str = "", tag = "option";
        for (i = start; i <= end; i += 1) {
            str += "<" + tag + " value='" + i + "'>" + i + "</" + tag + ">";
        }
        return str;
    }

    function getDistValues (has_miles) {
        var value, label;

        if (has_miles) {
            value = [5,10,20,50,75,100,200,300,500,1000,2000,3000,5000,10000];
            label = value;
        } else {
            value = [3,6,12,31,46,50,63,100,125,313,500,625,1000,1243,1864,3106,6214];
            label = [5,10,20,50,75,80,100,160,200,500,800,1000,1600,2000,3000,5000,10000];
        }

        return {value:value, label:label};
     }

    function getDistOptions (opts) {
        var distances,
            value,
            label,
            has_miles = g.country == "United States",
            measure = has_miles ? deftags.mile_text : deftags.km_text,
            str,
            i,
            l;
        opts = opts || {};
        str = '<option value="' + (opts.any || 99998) + '" data-label="' + deftags.any_text + ' ' + measure + '">' + deftags.any_text + '</option>';

        distances = getDistValues(has_miles);
        value = distances.value;
        label = distances.label;

        l = value.length;
        for (i = 0; i < l; i += 1) {
            str += '<option value="' + value[i] + '" data-label="' + label[i] + ' ' + measure + '">'+ label[i] + ' ' + measure + '</option>';
        }

        return str;
    }

    function getHeightOptions () {
        var i,
            l,
            value,
            str = "<option value='0' data-label='" + deftags.any_text + "'>" + deftags.any_text + "</option>",
            has_ft = g.country == "United States",
            measure = has_ft ? "" : " " + deftags.cm;

        if (g.country == "United States") {
            value = ['< 5 ft 0 in','5 ft 0 in','5 ft 1 in','5 ft 2 in','5 ft 3 in','5 ft 4 in','5 ft 5 in','5 ft 6 in','5 ft 7 in','5 ft 8 in','5 ft 9 in','5 ft 10 in','5 ft 11 in','6 ft 0 in','6 ft 1 in','6 ft 2 in','6 ft 3 in','6 ft 4 in',' > 6 ft 4 in'];
        } else {
            value = ['< 152','152-154','154-157','157-160','160-162','162-165','165-167','167-170','170-172','170-175','175-177','177-180','180-182','182-185','185-187','187-190','190-193','193-195','> 193'];
        }

        for (i = 0, l = value.length; i < l; i += 1) {
            str += "<option value='" + (i + 1) + "' data-label='" + value[i] + measure + "'>" + value[i] + measure + "</option>";
        }
        return str;
    }

    function getCountries (callback) {
        if (callback && typeof callback == 'function') {
            VIce.$.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: '/coreapi/form_element?action=country&_=' + new Date().getTime(),
                success: callback
            });
        }
    }

    function getMonths () {
        var str = "";
        _.each(deftags.months, function (m, i) {
            str += '<option value="' + (i + 1) + '">' + m + '</option>';
        });
        return str;
    }
    function getDays () {
        var i, str = "";
        for (i = 1; i < 32; i +=1) {
            str += '<option value="' + i + '">' + i + '</option>';
        }
        return str;
    }
    function getYears () {
        var str = "",
            l = new Date().getFullYear() - 21,
            i = l - 101;
        while (--l > i) {
            str += '<option value="' + l + '">' + l + '</option>';
        }
        return str;
    }
    g.getMonths = getMonths;
    g.getDays = getDays;
    g.getYears = getYears;
    g.getCountries = getCountries;
    g.getAgeOptions = getAgeOptions;
    g.getDistValues = getDistValues;
    g.getDistOptions = getDistOptions;
    g.getHeightOptions = getHeightOptions;
    g.sex = '';
}());

        } else if (href && g_name && g_name === "profile") {
            if (query_obj.pwsid) {
                href += "&p_pwsid=" + query_obj.pwsid;
            }


            if (p_col) {
                p_col.request = {
                    pwsid:query_obj.pwsid
                };

                p_col.next({trigger_only:1});
                
                p_col.on('add_complete', function(data){
                    if (parseInt(data.can_view, 10) > 0 || parseInt(data.i_am_fan_of_rank,10) === 1) {
                        changePageOld(section, page_name, query_obj, options);
                    } else {
                        window.location.href = href;
                    }
                    p_col.off('add_complete'); });
            } else {
                window.location.href = href;
            }
        }
    };

    if (g.show_adds) {
        
        g.$ad = VIce.$('[data-name="AdSpot"]');
        g.$ad_iframe = g.$ad ? g.$ad.find('iframe') : false;
        if (g.$ad_iframe.length && !g.adsfree) {
            g.ad_spots = {  'mc_message_page' : { spot:'https://medleyads.com/spot/19319.html' + g.medley_vars, href: "https://secure.adultfriendfinder.com/p/order.cgi?who=r,2AhpQWtbwUiKuOwPTBCNacvOlKyFYViKjVm85jQPKEXhMLlaQ2/yo28NM9kJCsk73mpY/RR5kz9vzqM0HwAbU5Rt/RKIyN3ytYIFqlLHhaQHUnYAJ1shuntEvY0bhwhwTHqo1TEdGYjz48IPYhD_fw--&site=ffadult&do_adsfree=1&origin=adsfree_mobile_mc" },
                            'mc_search' : { spot:'https://medleyads.com/spot/19319.html' + g.medley_vars, href: "https://secure.adultfriendfinder.com/p/order.cgi?who=r,2AhpQWtbwUiKuOwPTBCNacvOlKyFYViKjVm85jQPKEXhMLlaQ2/yo28NM9kJCsk73mpY/RR5kz9vzqM0HwAbU5Rt/RKIyN3ytYIFqlLHhaQHUnYAJ1shuntEvY0bhwhwTHqo1TEdGYjz48IPYhD_fw--&site=ffadult&do_adsfree=1&origin=adsfree_mobile_mc" },
                            'imc' : { spot: 'https://medleyads.com/spot/19320.html' + g.medley_vars, href: "https://secure.adultfriendfinder.com/p/order.cgi?who=r,2AhpQWtbwUiKuOwPTBCNacvOlKyFYViKjVm85jQPKEXhMLlaQ2/yo28NM9kJCsk73mpY/RR5kz9vzqM0HwAbU5Rt/RKIyN3ytYIFqlLHhaQHUnYAJ1shuntEvY0bhwhwTHqo1TEdGYjz48IPYhD_fw--&site=ffadult&do_adsfree=1&origin=adsfree_mobile_imc" },
                            'search_results' : { spot: 'https://medleyads.com/spot/19321.html' + g.medley_vars, href: "https://secure.adultfriendfinder.com/p/order.cgi?who=r,2AhpQWtbwUiKuOwPTBCNacvOlKyFYViKjVm85jQPKEXhMLlaQ2/yo28NM9kJCsk73mpY/RR5kz9vzqM0HwAbU5Rt/RKIyN3ytYIFqlLHhaQHUnYAJ1shuntEvY0bhwhwTHqo1TEdGYjz48IPYhD_fw--&site=ffadult&do_adsfree=1&origin=adsfree_mobile_search" },
                            'notifications' : { spot:'https://medleyads.com/spot/19322.html' + g.medley_vars, href: "https://secure.adultfriendfinder.com/p/order.cgi?who=r,2AhpQWtbwUiKuOwPTBCNacvOlKyFYViKjVm85jQPKEXhMLlaQ2/yo28NM9kJCsk73mpY/RR5kz9vzqM0HwAbU5Rt/RKIyN3ytYIFqlLHhaQHUnYAJ1shuntEvY0bhwhwTHqo1TEdGYjz48IPYhD_fw--&site=ffadult&do_adsfree=1&origin=adsfree_mobile_notifications" } };
            VIce.adSpots = (function(ad){
                var ad_src, old_w, oldResize = window.onresize, resize_db;
                function showUpsell () {
                    ad.closebar.hide();
                    ad.content.hide();
                    ad.upsell.show();
                    if (ad.old_os) {
                        ad.upsell[0].offsetHeight;
                    }
                    return false;
                }
                function showAd () {
                    ad.main.show();
                    ad.closebar.show();
                    ad.content.show();
                    ad.upsell.hide();
                    if (ad.old_os) {
                        ad.content[0].offsetHeight;
                    }
                }
                function removeAd () {
                    ad.main.hide();
                    g.adsfree = 1;
                    $.get(ad.pref_url.url, ad.pref_url.data); }
                
                function adOnPage () {
                    if (!g.adsfree && (ad_src = ad.spots[VIce.currentPage().name()])) {
                        if (!ad.old_os) {
                            ad.$iframe.attr('src', ad_src.spot);
                        }
                        ad.$order.attr('href', ad_src.href); resizeAd();
                    } else {
                        ad.main.hide();
                    }
                }
                function resizeAd () {
                    old_w = VIce.currentPage().innerWidth();
                    ad.main.show();
                    ad.$iframe.attr('height', old_w * 0.133);
                    ad.$iframe.attr('width', old_w);
                    
                    if (ad.old_os) {
                        ad.$iframe.attr('src', ad_src.spot);
                    }
                    showAd();
                }
                resize_db = _.debounce(resizeAd, 300);
                window.onresize = function () {
                    if ( ad_src && old_w != VIce.currentPage().innerWidth() ) {
                        ad.main.hide(); resize_db();
                    }
                    if (typeof oldResize === 'function') {
                        oldResize();
                    }
                };
                return {
                    adOnPage:adOnPage,
                    showUpsell:showUpsell,
                    showAd:showAd,
                    removeAd:removeAd
                };
            })({
                main : g.$ad,
                closebar : g.$ad.find('[data-name="AdClose"]'),
                content : g.$ad.find('[data-name="AdContent"]'),
                upsell : g.$ad.find('[data-name="AdUpsell"]'),
                $order : g.$ad.find('[data-name="AFOrder"]'),
                $iframe  : g.$ad_iframe,
                spots : g.ad_spots,
                old_os : VIce.$.support.isOsVersionOlder({'os':'android','version':'3.0'}),
                pref_url : {
                    url: '/p/update.cgi',
                    data : {
                        p:'my_account_update_ads_switch',
                        adsfree_preference:1,
                        ajax:1
                    }
                }
            });
            VIce.on('pagechanged', VIce.adSpots.adOnPage);
            g.$ad.on('click', '[data-name="AdClose"]', VIce.adSpots.showUpsell).on('click', '[data-name="AdShow"]', VIce.adSpots.showAd).on('click', '[data-name="AdRemove"]', VIce.adSpots.removeAd);
        }
    }
});

</script>

            <p class="wrapper">We are aware of a data security issue which appears to have affected a very small percentage of our users.  Unfortunately, your account WAS one of the accounts we believe to have been affected. At this time, there is no evidence that your personal financial information or your password have been compromised. To protect your privacy, we have hidden your original username from all users. Currently, no users can find you on the site. To ensure that the community can find you and interact with you again, <strong>you MUST update your username now</strong>.</p>

<script>
    (function(){
        var cont = document.createElement('div'),
            g = (window.VIce && VIce.globals) || {},
            other_lbs =  g.show_confirm_id || g.show_chat_credits,
            active_to,
            config = {
                active_time: 15000,
                and_txt: "Install this web app <img src=\"{{img}}\"> on your Android tap <img class=\"tta_more\" src=\"{{icon}}\"> and then <span class=\"tta_bold\">Add to Home Screen</span>",
                ios_txt: "Install this web app on your iPhone : tap <img src=\"{{icon}}\"> and then <span class=\"tta_bold\">Add to Home Screen.</span>",
                and_ico: "https://secureimage.securedataimages.com/images/ffadult/and_more.png",
                ios_ico: "https://secureimage.securedataimages.com/images/ffadult/ios_share.png",
                and_img: "https://secureimage.securedataimages.com/images/ffadult/aff_mobile_ico_18x18.png"
            };

        if (document.cookie.indexOf('hideatt') == -1 && !other_lbs) {
            addTTA();
        }

        function fadeOut() {
            cont.className += ' tta_fade';
        }

        function closeNotice(do_once) {
            var tomorrow = (new Date(+(new Date()) + (24*60*60*1000))).toGMTString(),
                eot = 'Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT';

            do_once = do_once || (this.getAttribute && this.getAttribute('data-once'));
            document.cookie = "hideatt=1; expires="
                + (do_once ? eot : tomorrow) + "; path=/";

            clearTimeout(active_to);
            fadeOut();
        }

        function addTTA() {
            var tta = document.getElementById('tta'),
                body = document.body || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0],
                close_btn,
                txt,
                i,
                ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase(),
                is_ios = /ipad|iphone|ipod/.test(ua) && /webkit/.test(ua) && !/crios\//.test(ua) && !window.MSStream,
                is_ipad = /ipad/.test(ua),
                is_chrome = /(chrome|crios)\//.test(ua);

            if (!is_ios && !is_chrome) {
                closeNotice(true);
                return;
            }

            cont.innerHTML = tta.innerHTML;

            if (is_ipad) {
                config.ios_txt = config.ios_txt.replace('','');
                config.ios_txt = config.ios_txt.replace('iPhone','iPad');
            }

            cont.className = is_ios? 'ios' + (is_ipad ? ' ipad' : '') : 'android';
            cont.setAttribute('id', 'tta');


            if (is_ios) {
                txt = config.ios_txt.replace('{{icon}}', config.ios_ico);
            } else {
                txt = config.and_txt.replace('{{icon}}', config.and_ico);
                txt = txt.replace('{{img}}', config.and_img);
            }

            cont.querySelector('[data-name="tta_txt"]').innerHTML = txt;

            close_btn = cont.getElementsByClassName('tta_close');

            i = close_btn.length;

            while(i--) {
                close_btn[i].onclick = closeNotice;
            }

            body.appendChild(cont);
            active_to = setTimeout(fadeOut, config.active_time);
        }
    })();
</script>

    <script>
    (function () {
        var VIce = window.VIce || {},
            menuBottom = VIce.$('#sticky-menu-button'),
            messageCenter = VIce.$('#message-center');

        var StickyNavBarMenu = (function () {
            var  imcCount = 0,
                 mcCount ='' || 0,
                 totalMsgs = 0,
                 mcDistributor = VIce.$('#imc-to-mc'),
                 imcChatboxPage = "#imc_chatbox",
                 mcConversationPage = "#mc_conversation_page",
                 replyPage = "#reply_page",
                 chatroomsDetails = "#chatrooms_details",
                 viewer = '#viewer',
                 profile = "#profile",
                 menuIconTab = VIce.$('.nav-tab-icon');


            function toggleRightMenu() {
                VIce.activateMenu();
            }

            function msgTabActivete(el) {
                VIce.$('.mct-outer').removeClass('active-tab');
                VIce.$('.mct-outer').each(function () {
                    if( VIce.$(this).attr('href') === el.attr('href')) {
                        VIce.$(this).addClass('active-tab');
                    }
                });
            }

            function activateNavTabClick() {
                var lastClicked;
                    menuIconTab.on('click', function () {
                        _this = VIce.$(this);
                        if (_this.attr('id') === 'imc-to-mc') {
                            msgTabActivete(_this);
                            messageCenter.show();
                        } else {
                            messageCenter.hide();
                        }
                        if(_this.hasClass('menu-nav-tab') && VIce.currentPage().menu_mode === 'off'){
                            menuIconTab.removeClass('active-tab');
                            if(lastClicked) {
                                lastClicked.addClass('active-tab');
                                if (lastClicked.attr('id') === 'imc-to-mc') {
                                    messageCenter.show();
                                }
                            }
                        } else {
                            menuIconTab.removeClass('active-tab');
                            _this.addClass('active-tab');
                        }

                        if(!_this.hasClass('menu-nav-tab')){
                            lastClicked = _this;
                        }
                    });
            }

            function activateNavTabLoad() {

                var urlStr = window.location.hash,
                    start_pos = urlStr.indexOf('#') + 1,
                    end_pos = urlStr.indexOf('?',start_pos);


                    if (end_pos === -1) {
                        end_pos = urlStr.length;
                    }
                    var urlClass = urlStr.substring(start_pos, end_pos);
                    menuIconTab.each(function () {
                        var _this = VIce.$(this);
                        if ( VIce.$(this).hasClass(urlClass)) {
                            VIce.$(this).addClass('active-tab');
                            if( VIce.$(this).attr('id') === "imc-to-mc") {
                                msgTabActivete(_this);
                                messageCenter.show();
                            }
                        }
                    });
            }

            function activeSearchProfile() {
                var urlStr = window.location.hash;
                 if (urlStr.indexOf(profile) !== -1) {
                        messageCenter.hide();
                        VIce.$('.nav-tab-icon').removeClass('active-tab');
                        VIce.$("#search-nav-tab").addClass('active-tab');
                    }
            }
