               data = data || {};
               var imUrl = '#imc?{"ga_key":"icon"}',
                   mcUrl = '/go/page/vice_cover.html?&who=r,2AhpQWtbwUiKuOwPTBCNacvOlKyFYViKjVm85jQPKEXhMLlaQ2/yo28NM9kJCsk73mpY/RR5kz9vzqM0HwAbU5Rt/RKIyN3ytYIFqlLHhaQHUnYAJ1shuntEvY0bhwhwTHqo1TEdGYjz48IPYhD_fw--#mc_message_page',
                   mcDistributorCountView = VIce.$('#imc-to-mc .unread_total_mc_imc'),
                   ls_key = VIce.globals.handle + "_imc_count",
                   count = 0;

                if (!isNaN(data.inbox_new_count) && isFinite(data.inbox_new_count)) {
                     count = data.inbox_new_count;
                } else if(!isNaN(data) && isFinite(data)) {
                    count = data;
                } else {
                    count = 0;
                }

                if(msg === 'imcCount') {
                    imcCount = count;
                } else if (msg === 'mcCount'){
                    mcCount = count;
                }

                imcCount = parseInt(imcCount, 10);
                try{
                  window.localStorage.setItem(ls_key,imcCount);
                }catch(e){
                }
                mcCount = parseInt(mcCount, 10);

                if (mcCount < imcCount) {
                    mcDistributor.attr('href', imUrl);
                } else {
                    mcDistributor.attr('href', mcUrl);
                }

                totalMsgs = imcCount + mcCount;

                if (totalMsgs) {
                    mcDistributorCountView.text(totalMsgs > 999 ? '999+' : totalMsgs);
                    mcDistributorCountView.show();
                } else {
                    mcDistributorCountView.hide();
                }
            }

            function handleMessageBar() {
                    VIce.on("mc_message_count", function (data) {
                         msgCounts(data, 'mcCount');
                     });
                    VIce.on("member_chat", function (data) {
                        msgCounts(data, 'imcCount');
                    });
            }

            function activateMsgTab() {
                var msgTab = VIce.$('#sticky-menu .mct-outer');
                    msgTab.on('click', function () {
                        _this = VIce.$(this);
                        msgTab.removeClass('active-tab');
                        _this.addClass('active-tab');
                    });
            }
            function toggleNavBar() {
                var leftButton = VIce.$('[data-role=header] [data-content=left_button]'),
                    urlStr = window.location.hash,
                    footerBody = VIce.$("div[data-content=footer_body]"),
                    stickyMenu = VIce.$('#sticky-menu');

                    if(urlStr.indexOf(imcChatboxPage) !== -1 || urlStr.indexOf(mcConversationPage) !== -1 || urlStr.indexOf(viewer) !== -1 || urlStr.indexOf(replyPage) !== -1 || urlStr.indexOf(chatroomsDetails) !== -1 ) {
                        footerBody.css('padding-bottom', '0');
                        leftButton.css('visibility', 'visible');
                        stickyMenu.hide();
                    } else if(urlStr.indexOf(profile) !== -1 && VIce.history.length > 0){
                        footerBody.css('padding-bottom', '0');
                        leftButton.css('visibility', 'visible');
                    } else {
                        stickyMenu.show();
                        footerBody.css('padding-bottom', '105px');
                        leftButton.css('visibility', 'hidden');
                    }
            }
            return {
                toggleRightMenu: toggleRightMenu,
                activateNavTabClick: activateNavTabClick,
                activateNavTabLoad: activateNavTabLoad,
                handleMessageBar: handleMessageBar,
                activateMsgTab: activateMsgTab,
                toggleNavBar: toggleNavBar,
                activeSearchProfile: activeSearchProfile
            }
        })();

        VIce.$.extend(VIce, StickyNavBarMenu);

        var navBarMenuInit = (function () {
            VIce.activateNavTabClick();
            VIce.handleMessageBar();
            VIce.activateNavTabLoad();
            VIce.activateMsgTab();
            menuBottom.on('click', VIce.toggleRightMenu);
            VIce.on('pagechanged', function () {
                VIce.toggleNavBar();
                VIce.activeSearchProfile();
            });

        })();
        VIce.$(document).ready(navBarMenuInit);
    })();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
